		#    #            #            #                #        #               #        #
#########    #            #########    #########    #########    #           #########    #########
#BORMANN SIG SPECIFIC EFFECTS


# Index - assuming you're not Lamounier and remember which SIG is which by the back of your hand.
# 0 - Party Bureaucracy
# 1 - People
# 2 - Intelligentsia
# 3 - Church
# 4 - Heer
# 5 - Kriegsmarine
# 6 - Ordnungspolizei
# 7 - Reichswerke
# 8 - IG Farben
# 9 - Siemens
# 10 - Slave Plantations
# 11 - The Banks

# Specific reading index:
# BOR_SIG_[AP/SP/AL/SL]_[SIG index]_[value]_[Faction index (if using AL/SL)]
# AP - Add Power - values: (1/2/3/4/5/10/20)
# SP - Subtract Power - values: (1/2/3/4/5/10/20)
# AL - Add Loyalty - values: (1/2/3/4/5/6)
# SL - Subtract Loyalty - values: (1/2/3/4/5/6)

# Faction support index:
# BOR_SIG_[AS/SS]_[Faction index]_[value]
# AS - Add Support - values: (1/2/3/4/5/10/20/25/30)
# SS - Subtract Support - values: (1/2/3/4/5/10/20/25/30)

# Faction index:
# 0 - Reformists
# 1 - Conservatives
# 2 - Militarists

# Example:
# BOR_SIG_AP_11_20 adds 20 power to the banks (SIG Index 11)
# BOR_SIG_SL_3_5_2 subtracts 5% militarists loyalty from church (SIG Index 3)
# BOR_SIG_AS_0_25 adds 25% reformist faction support to the government

###################
###  ADD POWER  ###
###################

#####  SIG 0  #####
BOR_SIG_AP_0_1 = {
	log = "BOR_SIG_AP_0_1; executing."
	custom_effect_tooltip = BOR_SIG_AP_0_1_tt
	set_country_flag = BOR_SIG_specific_effect
	set_variable = { BOR_SIG_AP_i = 0 }
	set_variable = { BOR_SIG_AP_v = 1 }
	BOR_SIG_AddPower = yes
	log = "BOR_SIG_AP_0_1; completed execution."
}
